\"symbol\": \"getFactory\"\n    },\n    {\n      \"repo\": \"github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2\",\n      \"path\": \"envoy/registry/registry.h\",\n      \"symbol\": \"getFactoryByType\"\n    },\n Pattern Implementation\\n\\nThe Envoy proxy implements an extension registry pattern that enables dynamic, compile-time discovery and registration of extension factories. The architecture consists of several key components:\\n\\n### Core Components\\n\\n**1. Registry Template Class (envoy/registry/registry.h:166)**\\nThe `FactoryRegistry<Base>` template class is the central registry that manages all factory instances for a given base class. It maintains:\\n- A static factory map (hash map from name to factory pointer)\\n- Factories indexed by configuration type\\n- Versioning information for vendor-specific factories\\n- Deprecated factory name mappings\\n\\nKey methods:\\n- `getFactory(name)` - Lookup factory by string name\\n- `getFactoryByType(type_url)` - Lookup by protobuf type\\n- `registerFactory(Base& factory, absl::string_view name)` - Runtime registration\\n- `registeredNames()` - List all registered factories\\n\\n**2. RegisterFactory Template Class (envoy/registry/registry.h:507)**\\nThe `RegisterFactory<T, Base>` template enables static registration of factory instances. When instantiated (typically at module load time), the constructor:\\n1. Creates a static instance of the concrete factory (T)\\n2. Registers it with `FactoryRegistry<Base>::registerFactory()`\\n3. Registers the factory's category with `FactoryCategoryRegistry`\\n\\nThe RegisterFactory constructor supports multiple overloads for:\\n- Basic registration\\n- Registration with deprecated names\\n- Registration with vendor-specific versions (major, minor, patch)\\n\\n**3. Macros (envoy/registry/registry.h:618-654)**\\nTwo macro variants handle static registration:\\n\\n`REGISTER_FACTORY(FACTORY, BASE)` - When `ENVOY_STATIC_EXTENSION_REGISTRATION` is defined:\\n```cpp\\nstatic Envoy::Registry::RegisterFactory<FACTORY, BASE> FACTORY##_registered;\\n```\\n\\nWhen not defined, it generates a function that dynamically creates the RegisterFactory:\\n```cpp\\nvoid forceRegister##FACTORY() {\\n  static auto registered = new Envoy::Registry::RegisterFactory<FACTORY, BASE>();\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**4. Factory Base Classes (envoy/config/typed_config.h)**\\n- `UntypedFactory` - Base with `name()` and `category()` methods\\n- `TypedFactory` - Extends UntypedFactory with `createEmptyConfigProto()` for protobuf configuration\\n\\n### Self-Registration at Static Initialization\\n\\nThe pattern leverages C++ static initialization to register factories:\\n\\n1. **Compile-time registration** (typical): Extensions define a static instance of `RegisterFactory<ConcreteFactory, BaseFactory>` at file scope, which runs during program initialization.\\n\\n2. **Example from source/extensions/filters/http/geoip/config.cc:35-36**:\\n```cpp\\nREGISTER_FACTORY(GeoipFilterFactory,\\n                 Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory){\\\"envoy.geoip\\\"};\\n```\\nThis expands to a static `RegisterFactory` instance that registers `GeoipFilterFactory` under the name \\\"envoy.geoip\\\".\\n\\n3. **Factory Category Registry**: Each factory also registers its category string (`UntypedFactory::category()` method) with `FactoryCategoryRegistry`, enabling discovery by category.\\n\\n### Factory Lookup Pattern\\n\\nAt runtime, extensions are discovered via two mechanisms:\\n\\n1. **By name lookup** (envoy/registry/registry.h:293):\\n```cpp\\nBase* getFactory(absl::string_view name) {\\n  auto it = factories().find(name);\\n  return (it == factories().end()) ? nullptr : it->second;\\n}\\n```\\n\\n2. **By protobuf type** (envoy/registry/registry.h:302):\\nThe `factoriesByType()` map is lazily built from all registered factories' `configTypes()`, enabling type-based lookup.\\n\\n### Configuration Implementation Files\\n\\n**Context and Utility Files:**\\n- `source/server/factory_context_impl.h` - FactoryContextImplBase for factory creation contexts\\n- `source/server/configuration_impl.h` - StatsSinkFactory and configuration management\\n- `source/common/config/utility.h` - Utility functions like `getAndCheckFactoryByName()` and `translateToFactoryConfig()`\\n\\n**Test Utilities (test/test_common/registry.h):**\\n- `InjectFactory<Base>` - Temporarily replaces a factory for testing\\n- `InjectFactoryCategory<Base>` - Registers a test category\\n\\n### Extension Implementation Pattern\\n\\nEach extension (found throughout source/extensions/) implements this pattern:\\n\\n1. **Header file** (e.g., config.h): Defines a factory class inheriting from `Config::TypedFactory` or base class specific to that extension type\\n2. **Implementation file** (e.g., config.cc): \\n   - Implements `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` or equivalent\\n   - Uses `REGISTER_FACTORY` macro at file scope for static registration\\n   - Looks up other factories via `Registry::FactoryRegistry<T>::getFactory()`\\n\\nExamples of this pattern appear in:\\n- HTTP filters (geoip, grpc_web, wasm, connect_grpc_bridge)\\n- Listener filters (tls_inspector, http_inspector, original_dst, proxy_protocol)\\n- Access loggers (fluentd, open_telemetry, stream)\\n- Tracers (opentelemetry, skywalking)\\n- Load balancing policies (maglev, cluster_provided)\\n- Stat sinks (dog_statsd, hystrix)\\n- And many more (48+ files in source/extensions/)\\n\\n### Thread Safety\\n\\nThe registry is **not thread-safe** during registration. Registration must occur in a single-threaded environment, guaranteed by static initialization happening before main() executes. All factory lookups after initialization are safe for concurrent access since the maps are only read, not modified.\\n\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2001,"cache_read_input_tokens":83101,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2001},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"07543747-7fa8-48e8-a9b4-c7aafe99e866","uuid":"e77ab6cb-300e-4251-ae9d-da9efa7eb82b"}

The architecture consists of several key components:\\n\\n### Core Components\\n\\n**1. \"text\": \"## Envoy Extension Registry Pattern Implementation\\n\\nThe Envoy proxy implements an extension registry pattern that enables dynamic, compile-time discovery and registration of extension factories. The architecture consists of several key components:\\n\\n### Core Components\\n\\n**1. Registry Template Class (envoy/registry/registry.h:166)**\\nThe `FactoryRegistry<Base>` template class is the central registry that manages all factory instances for a given base class. It maintains:\\n- A static factory map (hash map from name to factory pointer)\\n- Factories indexed by configuration type\\n- Versioning information for vendor-specific factories\\n- Deprecated factory name mappings\\n\\nKey methods:\\n- `getFactory(name)` - Lookup factory by string name\\n- `getFactoryByType(type_url)` - Lookup by protobuf type\\n- `registerFactory(Base& factory, absl::string_view name)` - Runtime registration\\n- `registeredNames()` - List all registered factories\\n\\n**2. RegisterFactory Template Class (envoy/registry/registry.h:507)**\\nThe `RegisterFactory<T, Base>` template enables static registration of factory instances. When instantiated (typically at module load time), the constructor:\\n1. Creates a static instance of the concrete factory (T)\\n2. Registers it with `FactoryRegistry<Base>::registerFactory()`\\n3. Registers the factory's category with `FactoryCategoryRegistry`\\n\\nThe RegisterFactory constructor supports multiple overloads for:\\n- Basic registration\\n- Registration with deprecated names\\n- Registration with vendor-specific versions (major, minor, patch)\\n\\n**3. Macros (envoy/registry/registry.h:618-654)**\\nTwo macro variants handle static registration:\\n\\n`REGISTER_FACTORY(FACTORY, BASE)` - When `ENVOY_STATIC_EXTENSION_REGISTRATION` is defined:\\n```cpp\\nstatic Envoy::Registry::RegisterFactory<FACTORY, BASE> FACTORY##_registered;\\n```\\n\\nWhen not defined, it generates a function that dynamically creates the RegisterFactory:\\n```cpp\\nvoid forceRegister##FACTORY() {\\n  static auto registered = new Envoy::Registry::RegisterFactory<FACTORY, BASE>();\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**4. Factory Base Classes (envoy/config/typed_config.h)**\\n- `UntypedFactory` - Base with `name()` and `category()` methods\\n- `TypedFactory` - Extends UntypedFactory with `createEmptyConfigProto()` for protobuf configuration\\n\\n### Self-Registration at Static Initialization\\n\\nThe pattern leverages C++ static initialization to register factories:\\n\\n1. **Compile-time registration** (typical): Extensions define a static instance of `RegisterFactory<ConcreteFactory, BaseFactory>` at file scope, which runs during program initialization.\\n\\n2. **Example from source/extensions/filters/http/geoip/config.cc:35-36**:\\n```cpp\\nREGISTER_FACTORY(GeoipFilterFactory,\\n                 Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory){\\\"envoy.geoip\\\"};\\n```\\nThis expands to a static `RegisterFactory` instance that registers `GeoipFilterFactory` under the name \\\"envoy.geoip\\\".\\n\\n3. **Factory Category Registry**: Each factory also registers its category string (`UntypedFactory::category()` method) with `FactoryCategoryRegistry`, enabling discovery by category.\\n\\n### Factory Lookup Pattern\\n\\nAt runtime, extensions are discovered via two mechanisms:\\n\\n1. **By name lookup** (envoy/registry/registry.h:293):\\n```cpp\\nBase* getFactory(absl::string_view name) {\\n  auto it = factories().find(name);\\n  return (it == factories().end()) ? nullptr : it->second;\\n}\\n```\\n\\n2. **By protobuf type** (envoy/registry/registry.h:302):\\nThe `factoriesByType()` map is lazily built from all registered factories' `configTypes()`, enabling type-based lookup.\\n\\n### Configuration Implementation Files\\n\\n**Context and Utility Files:**\\n- `source/server/factory_context_impl.h` - FactoryContextImplBase for factory creation contexts\\n- `source/server/configuration_impl.h` - StatsSinkFactory and configuration management\\n- `source/common/config/utility.h` - Utility functions like `getAndCheckFactoryByName()` and `translateToFactoryConfig()`\\n\\n**Test Utilities (test/test_common/registry.h):**\\n- `InjectFactory<Base>` - Temporarily replaces a factory for testing\\n- `InjectFactoryCategory<Base>` - Registers a test category\\n\\n### Extension Implementation Pattern\\n\\nEach extension (found throughout source/extensions/) implements this pattern:\\n\\n1. **Header file** (e.g., config.h): Defines a factory class inheriting from `Config::TypedFactory` or base class specific to that extension type\\n2. **Implementation file** (e.g., config.cc): \\n   - Implements `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` or equivalent\\n   - Uses `REGISTER_FACTORY` macro at file scope for static registration\\n   - Looks up other factories via `Registry::FactoryRegistry<T>::getFactory()`\\n\\nExamples of this pattern appear in:\\n- HTTP filters (geoip, grpc_web, wasm, connect_grpc_bridge)\\n- Listener filters (tls_inspector, http_inspector, original_dst, proxy_protocol)\\n- Access loggers (fluentd, open_telemetry, stream)\\n- Tracers (opentelemetry, skywalking)\\n- Load balancing policies (maglev, cluster_provided)\\n- Stat sinks (dog_statsd, hystrix)\\n- And many more (48+ files in source/extensions/)\\n\\n### Thread Safety\\n\\nThe registry is **not thread-safe** during registration. Registration must occur in a single-threaded environment, guaranteed by static initialization happening before main() executes. All factory lookups after initialization are safe for concurrent access since the maps are only read, not modified.\\n\"\n   263→}\n   264→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. Pattern Implementation\\n\\nThe Envoy proxy implements an extension registry pattern that enables dynamic, compile-time discovery and registration of extension factories. The architecture consists of several key components:\\n\\n### Core Components\\n\\n**1. Registry Template Class (envoy/registry/registry.h:166)**\\nThe `FactoryRegistry<Base>` template class is the central registry that manages all factory instances for a given base class. It maintains:\\n- A static factory map (hash map from name to factory pointer)\\n- Factories indexed by configuration type\\n- Versioning information for vendor-specific factories\\n- Deprecated factory name mappings\\n\\nKey methods:\\n- `getFactory(name)` - Lookup factory by string name\\n- `getFactoryByType(type_url)` - Lookup by protobuf type\\n- `registerFactory(Base& factory, absl::string_view name)` - Runtime registration\\n- `registeredNames()` - List all registered factories\\n\\n**2. RegisterFactory Template Class (envoy/registry/registry.h:507)**\\nThe `RegisterFactory<T, Base>` template enables static registration of factory instances. When instantiated (typically at module load time), the constructor:\\n1. Creates a static instance of the concrete factory (T)\\n2. Registers it with `FactoryRegistry<Base>::registerFactory()`\\n3. Registers the factory's category with `FactoryCategoryRegistry`\\n\\nThe RegisterFactory constructor supports multiple overloads for:\\n- Basic registration\\n- Registration with deprecated names\\n- Registration with vendor-specific versions (major, minor, patch)\\n\\n**3. Macros (envoy/registry/registry.h:618-654)**\\nTwo macro variants handle static registration:\\n\\n`REGISTER_FACTORY(FACTORY, BASE)` - When `ENVOY_STATIC_EXTENSION_REGISTRATION` is defined:\\n```cpp\\nstatic Envoy::Registry::RegisterFactory<FACTORY, BASE> FACTORY##_registered;\\n```\\n\\nWhen not defined, it generates a function that dynamically creates the RegisterFactory:\\n```cpp\\nvoid forceRegister##FACTORY() {\\n  static auto registered = new Envoy::Registry::RegisterFactory<FACTORY, BASE>();\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**4. Factory Base Classes (envoy/config/typed_config.h)**\\n- `UntypedFactory` - Base with `name()` and `category()` methods\\n- `TypedFactory` - Extends UntypedFactory with `createEmptyConfigProto()` for protobuf configuration\\n\\n### Self-Registration at Static Initialization\\n\\nThe pattern leverages C++ static initialization to register factories:\\n\\n1. **Compile-time registration** (typical): Extensions define a static instance of `RegisterFactory<ConcreteFactory, BaseFactory>` at file scope, which runs during program initialization.\\n\\n2. **Example from source/extensions/filters/http/geoip/config.cc:35-36**:\\n```cpp\\nREGISTER_FACTORY(GeoipFilterFactory,\\n                 Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory){\\\"envoy.geoip\\\"};\\n```\\nThis expands to a static `RegisterFactory` instance that registers `GeoipFilterFactory` under the name \\\"envoy.geoip\\\".\\n\\n3. **Factory Category Registry**: Each factory also registers its category string (`UntypedFactory::category()` method) with `FactoryCategoryRegistry`, enabling discovery by category.\\n\\n### Factory Lookup Pattern\\n\\nAt runtime, extensions are discovered via two mechanisms:\\n\\n1. **By name lookup** (envoy/registry/registry.h:293):\\n```cpp\\nBase* getFactory(absl::string_view name) {\\n  auto it = factories().find(name);\\n  return (it == factories().end()) ? nullptr : it->second;\\n}\\n```\\n\\n2. **By protobuf type** (envoy/registry/registry.h:302):\\nThe `factoriesByType()` map is lazily built from all registered factories' `configTypes()`, enabling type-based lookup.\\n\\n### Configuration Implementation Files\\n\\n**Context and Utility Files:**\\n- `source/server/factory_context_impl.h` - FactoryContextImplBase for factory creation contexts\\n- `source/server/configuration_impl.h` - StatsSinkFactory and configuration management\\n- `source/common/config/utility.h` - Utility functions like `getAndCheckFactoryByName()` and `translateToFactoryConfig()`\\n\\n**Test Utilities (test/test_common/registry.h):**\\n- `InjectFactory<Base>` - Temporarily replaces a factory for testing\\n- `InjectFactoryCategory<Base>` - Registers a test category\\n\\n### Extension Implementation Pattern\\n\\nEach extension (found throughout source/extensions/) implements this pattern:\\n\\n1. **Header file** (e.g., config.h): Defines a factory class inheriting from `Config::TypedFactory` or base class specific to that extension type\\n2. **Implementation file** (e.g., config.cc): \\n   - Implements `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` or equivalent\\n   - Uses `REGISTER_FACTORY` macro at file scope for static registration\\n   - Looks up other factories via `Registry::FactoryRegistry<T>::getFactory()`\\n\\nExamples of this pattern appear in:\\n- HTTP filters (geoip, grpc_web, wasm, connect_grpc_bridge)\\n- Listener filters (tls_inspector, http_inspector, original_dst, proxy_protocol)\\n- Access loggers (fluentd, open_telemetry, stream)\\n- Tracers (opentelemetry, skywalking)\\n- Load balancing policies (maglev, cluster_provided)\\n- Stat sinks (dog_statsd, hystrix)\\n- And many more (48+ files in source/extensions/)\\n\\n### Thread Safety\\n\\nThe registry is **not thread-safe** during registration. Registration must occur in a single-threaded environment, guaranteed by static initialization happening before main() executes. All factory lookups after initialization are safe for concurrent access since the maps are only read, not modified.\\n\"\n}\n","numLines":264,"startLine":1,"totalLines":264}}}
